Otherwise, false\n     */\n    public static boolean waitForAllToComplete(List<Future<?>> jobs, Consumer<Throwable> callback) {\n        List<Future<?>> failed = new ArrayList<>();\n        for (Future<?> job : jobs) {\n            try {\n                job.get();\n            } catch (Exception e) {\n                callback.accept(e);\n                failed.add(job);\n            }\n        }\n        return failed.isEmpty();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns true if the given log should not be on the current broker\n     * according to the metadata image.\n     *\n     * @param brokerId       The ID of the current broker.\n     * @param newTopicsImage The new topics image after broker has been reloaded\n     * @param log            The log object to check\n     * @return true if the log should not exist on the broker, false otherwise.\n     */\n    public static boolean isStrayKraftReplica(int brokerId, TopicsImage newTopicsImage, UnifiedLog log) {\n        if (log.topicId().isEmpty()) {\n            // Missing topic ID could result from storage failure or unclean shutdown after topic creation but before flushing\n            // data to the `partition.metadata` file. And before appending data to the log, the `partition.metadata` is always\n            // flushed to disk. So if the topic ID is missing, it mostly means no data was appended, and we can treat this as\n            // a stray log.\n            LOG.info(\"The topicId does not exist in {}, treat it as a stray log.\", log);\n            return true;\n        }\n\n        Uuid topicId = log.topicId().get();\n        int partitionId = log.topicPartition().partition();\n        PartitionRegistration partition = newTopicsImage.getPartition(topicId, partitionId);\n        if (partition == null) {\n            LOG.info(\"Found stray log dir {}: the topicId {} does not exist in the metadata image.\", log, topicId);\n            return true;\n        } else {\n            List<Integer> replicas = Arrays.stream(partition.replicas).boxed().toList();\n            if (!replicas.contains(brokerId)) {\n                LOG.info(\"Found stray log dir {}: the current replica assignment {} does not contain the local brokerId {}.\",\n                        log, replicas.stream().map(String::valueOf).collect(Collectors.joining(\", \", \"[\", \"]\")), brokerId);\n                return true;\n            } else {\n                return false;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n","numLines":97,"startLine":1,"totalLines":97}}}

final int maxMessageSize;\n   291→    private final Map<?, ?> props;\n   292→\n   293→    public LogConfig(Map<?, ?> props) {\n   294→        this(props, Set.of());\n   295→    }\n   296→\n   297→    @SuppressWarnings({\"this-escape\"})\n   298→    public LogConfig(Map<?, ?> props, Set<String> overriddenConfigs) {\n   299→        super(CONFIG, props, false);\n   300→        this.props = Collections.unmodifiableMap(props);\n   301→        this.overriddenConfigs = Collections.unmodifiableSet(overriddenConfigs);\n   302→\n   303→        this.segmentSize = 306→        this.segmentJitterMs = getLong(TopicConfig.SEGMENT_JITTER_MS_CONFIG);\n   307→        this.maxIndexSize = getInt(TopicConfig.SEGMENT_INDEX_BYTES_CONFIG);\n   308→        this.flushInterval = getLong(TopicConfig.FLUSH_MESSAGES_INTERVAL_CONFIG);\n   309→        this.flushMs = getLong(TopicConfig.FLUSH_MS_CONFIG);\n   310→        this.retentionSize = getLong(TopicConfig.RETENTION_BYTES_CONFIG);\n   311→        this.retentionMs = getLong(TopicConfig.RETENTION_MS_CONFIG);\n   312→        this.maxMessageSize = getInt(TopicConfig.MAX_MESSAGE_BYTES_CONFIG);\n   313→        this.indexInterval = getInt(TopicConfig.INDEX_INTERVAL_BYTES_CONFIG);\n   314→        this.fileDeleteDelayMs = getLong(TopicConfig.FILE_DELETE_DELAY_MS_CONFIG);\n   315→        this.deleteRetentionMs = getLong(TopicConfig.DELETE_RETENTION_MS_CONFIG);\n   316→        this.compactionLagMs = getLong(TopicConfig.MIN_COMPACTION_LAG_MS_CONFIG);\n   317→        this.maxCompactionLagMs = getLong(TopicConfig.MAX_COMPACTION_LAG_MS_CONFIG);\n   318→        this.minCleanableRatio = getDouble(TopicConfig.MIN_CLEANABLE_DIRTY_RATIO_CONFIG);\n   319→        this.compact = getList(TopicConfig.CLEANUP_POLICY_CONFIG).stream()\n   320→                .map(c -> c.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))\n   321→                .toList()\n   322→                .contains(TopicConfig.CLEANUP_POLICY_COMPACT);\n   323→        this.delete = getList(TopicConfig.CLEANUP_POLICY_CONFIG).stream()\n   324→                .map(c -> c.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))\n   325→                .toList()\n   326→                .contains(TopicConfig.CLEANUP_POLICY_DELETE);\n   327→        this.uncleanLeaderElectionEnable = getBoolean(TopicConfig.UNCLEAN_LEADER_ELECTION_ENABLE_CONFIG);\n   328→        this.minInSyncReplicas = getInt(TopicConfig.MIN_IN_SYNC_REPLICAS_CONFIG);\n   329→        this.compressionType = BrokerCompressionType.forName(getString(TopicConfig.COMPRESSION_TYPE_CONFIG));\n   330→        this.compression = getCompression();\n   331→        this.preallocate = getBoolean(TopicConfig.PREALLOCATE_CONFIG);\n   332→        this.messageTimestampType = TimestampType.forName(getString(TopicConfig.MESSAGE_TIMESTAMP_TYPE_CONFIG));\n   333→        this.messageTimestampBeforeMaxMs = getLong(TopicConfig.MESSAGE_TIMESTAMP_BEFORE_MAX_MS_CONFIG);\n   334→        this.messageTimestampAfterMaxMs = getLong(TopicConfig.MESSAGE_TIMESTAMP_AFTER_MAX_MS_CONFIG);\n   335→        this.leaderReplicationThrottledReplicas = Collections.unmodifiableList(getList(QuotaConfig.LEADER_REPLICATION_THROTTLED_REPLICAS_CONFIG));\n   336→        this.followerReplicationThrottledReplicas = Collections.unmodifiableList(getList(QuotaConfig.FOLLOWER_REPLICATION_THROTTLED_REPLICAS_CONFIG));\n   337→\n   338→        remoteLogConfig = new RemoteLogConfig(this);\n   339→    }\n   340→\n   341→    private Optional<Compression> getCompression() {\n   342→        switch (compressionType) {\n   343→            case GZIP:\n   344→                return Optional.of(Compression.gzip()\n   345→                        .level(getInt(TopicConfig.COMPRESSION_GZIP_LEVEL_CONFIG))\n   346→                        .build());\n   347→            case LZ4:\n   348→                return Optional.of(Compression.lz4()\n   349→                        .level(getInt(TopicConfig.COMPRESSION_LZ4_LEVEL_CONFIG))\n   350→                        .build());\n   351→            case ZSTD:\n   352→                return Optional.of(Compression.zstd()\n   353→                        .level(getInt(TopicConfig.COMPRESSION_ZSTD_LEVEL_CONFIG))\n   354→                        .build());\n   355→            case SNAPPY:\n   356→                return Optional.of(Compression.snappy().build());\n   357→            case UNCOMPRESSED:\n   358→                return Optional.of(Compression.NONE);\n   359→            case PRODUCER:\n   360→                return Optional.empty();\n   361→            default:\n   362→                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid value for \" + TopicConfig.COMPRESSION_TYPE_CONFIG);\n   363→        }\n   364→    }\n   365→\n   366→    public int segmentSize() {\n   367→        if (internalSegmentSize == null) return segmentSize;\n   368→        return internalSegmentSize;\n   369→    }\n   370→\n   371→    // Exposed as a method so it can be mocked\n   372→    public int maxMessageSize() {\n   373→        return maxMessageSize;\n   374→    }\n   375→\n   376→    public long randomSegmentJitter() {\n   377→        if (segmentJitterMs == 0)\n   378→            return 0;\n   379→        else\n   380→            return Utils.abs(ThreadLocalRandom.current().nextInt()) % Math.min(segmentJitterMs, segmentMs);\n   381→    }\n   382→\n   383→    public long maxSegmentMs() {\n   384→        if (compact && maxCompactionLagMs > 0)\n   385→            return Math.min(maxCompactionLagMs, segmentMs);\n   386→        else\n   387→            return segmentMs;\n   388→    }\n   389→\n   390→    public int initFileSize() {\n   391→        if (preallocate)\n   392→            return segmentSize();\n   393→        else\n   394→            return 0;\n   395→    }\n   396→\n   397→    public boolean remoteStorageEnable() {\n   398→        return remoteLogConfig.remoteStorageEnable;\n   399→    }\n   400→\n   401→    public Boolean remoteLogDeleteOnDisable() {\n   402→        return remoteLogConfig.remoteLogDeleteOnDisable;\n   403→    }\n   404→\n   405→    public Boolean remoteLogCopyDisable() {\n   406→        return remoteLogConfig.remoteLogCopyDisable;\n   407→    }\n   408→\n   409→    public long localRetentionMs() {\n   410→        return remoteLogConfig.localRetentionMs == LogConfig.DEFAULT_LOCAL_RETENTION_MS ? retentionMs : remoteLogConfig.localRetentionMs;\n   411→    }\n   412→\n   413→    public long localRetentionBytes() {\n   414→        return remoteLogConfig.localRetentionBytes == LogConfig.DEFAULT_LOCAL_RETENTION_BYTES ? retentionSize : remoteLogConfig.localRetentionBytes;\n   415→    }\n   416→\n   417→    public String overriddenConfigsAsLoggableString() {\n   418→        Map<String, Object> overriddenTopicProps = new HashMap<>();\n   419→        props.forEach((k, v) -> {\n   420→            if (overriddenConfigs.contains(k))\n   421→                overriddenTopicProps.put((String) k, v);\n   422→        });\n   423→        return ConfigUtils.configMapToRedactedString(overriddenTopicProps, CONFIG);\n   424→    }\n   425→\n   426→    /**\n   427→     * Create a log config instance using the given properties and defaults\n   428→     */\n   429→    public static LogConfig fromProps(Map<?, ?> defaults, Properties overrides) {\n   430→        Properties props = new Properties();\n   431→        props.putAll(defaults);\n   432→        props.putAll(overrides);\n   433→        Set<String> overriddenKeys = overrides.keySet().stream().map(k -> (String) k).collect(Collectors.toSet());\n   434→        return new LogConfig(props, overriddenKeys);\n   435→    }\n   436→\n   437→    // Visible for testing, return a copy since it's a mutable global variable\n   438→    public static LogConfigDef configDefCopy() {\n   439→        return new LogConfigDef(CONFIG);\n   440→    }\n   441→\n   442→    public static Optional<Type> configType(String configName) {\n   443→        return Optional.ofNullable(CONFIG.configKeys().get(configName)).map(c -> c.type);\n   444→    }\n   445→\n   446→    public static List<String> configNames() {\n   447→        return CONFIG.names().stream().sorted().toList();\n   448→    }\n   449→\n   450→    public static List<String> nonInternalConfigNames() {\n   451→        return CONFIG.configKeys().entrySet()\n   452→                .stream()\n   453→                .filter(entry -> !entry.getValue().internalConfig)\n   454→                .map(Map.Entry::getKey)\n   455→                .sorted().toList();\n   456→    }\n   457→\n   458→    public static Map<String, ConfigKey> configKeys() {\n   459→        return Collections.unmodifiableMap(CONFIG.configKeys());\n   460→    }\n   461→\n   462→    /**\n   463→     * Check that property names are valid\n   464→     */\n   465→    public static void validateNames(Properties props) {\n   466→        List<String> names = configNames();\n   467→        for (Object name : props.keySet())\n   468→            if (!names.contains(name))\n   469→                throw new InvalidConfigurationException(\"Unknown topic config name: \" + name);\n   470→    }\n   471→\n   472→    /**\n   473→     * Validates the values of the given properties. Can be called by both client and server.\n   474→     * The `props` supplied should contain all the LogConfig properties and the default values are extracted from the\n   475→     * LogConfig class.\n   476→     * @param props The properties to be validated\n   477→     */\n   478→    public static void validateValues(Map<?, ?> props) {\n   479→        long minCompactionLag = (Long) props.get(TopicConfig.MIN_COMPACTION_LAG_MS_CONFIG);\n   480→        long maxCompactionLag = (Long) props.get(TopicConfig.MAX_COMPACTION_LAG_MS_CONFIG);\n   481→        if (minCompactionLag > maxCompactionLag) {\n   482→            throw new InvalidConfigurationException(\"conflict topic config setting \"\n   483→                    + TopicConfig.MIN_COMPACTION_LAG_MS_CONFIG + \" (\" + minCompactionLag + \") > \"\n   484→                    + TopicConfig.MAX_COMPACTION_LAG_MS_CONFIG + \" (\" + maxCompactionLag + \")\");\n   485→        }\n   486→    }\n   487→\n   488→    /**\n   489→     * Validates the values of the given properties. Should be called only by the broker.\n   490→     * The `props` supplied doesn't contain any topic-level configs, only broker-level configs.\n   491→     * The default values should be extracted from the KafkaConfig.\n   492→     * @param props The properties to be validated\n   493→     */\n   494→    public static void validateBrokerLogConfigValues(Map<?, ?> props,\n   495→                                                     boolean isRemoteLogStorageSystemEnabled) {\n   496→        validateValues(props);\n   497→        if (isRemoteLogStorageSystemEnabled) {\n   498→            validateRemoteStorageRetentionSize(props);\n   499→            validateRemoteStorageRetentionTime(props);\n   500→        }\n   501→    }\n   502→\n   503→    /**\n   504→     * Validates the values of the given properties. Should be called only by the broker.\n   505→     * The `newConfigs` supplied contains the topic-level configs,\n   506→     * The default values should be extracted from the KafkaConfig.\n   507→     * @param existingConfigs                   The existing properties\n   508→     * @param newConfigs                        The new properties to be validated\n   509→     * @param isRemoteLogStorageSystemEnabled   true if system wise remote log storage is enabled\n   510→     */\n   511→    private static void validateTopicLogConfigValues(Map<String, String> existingConfigs,\n   512→                                                     Map<?, ?> newConfigs,\n   513→                                                     boolean isRemoteLogStorageSystemEnabled) {\n   514→        validateValues(newConfigs);\n   515→\n   516→        boolean isRemoteLogStorageEnabled = (Boolean) newConfigs.get(TopicConfig.REMOTE_LOG_STORAGE_ENABLE_CONFIG);\n   517→        if (isRemoteLogStorageEnabled) {\n   518→            validateRemoteStorageOnlyIfSystemEnabled(newConfigs, isRemoteLogStorageSystemEnabled, false);\n   519→            validateRemoteStorageRequiresDeleteCleanupPolicy(newConfigs);\n   520→            validateRemoteStorageRetentionSize(newConfigs);\n   521→            validateRemoteStorageRetentionTime(newConfigs);\n   522→            validateRetentionConfigsWhenRemoteCopyDisabled(newConfigs, isRemoteLogStorageEnabled);\n   523→        } else {\n   524→            // The new config \"remote.storage.enable\" is getCompression() {\n        switch (compressionType) {\n            case GZIP:\n                return Optional.of(Compression.gzip()\n                        .level(getInt(TopicConfig.COMPRESSION_GZIP_LEVEL_CONFIG))\n                        .build());\n            case LZ4:\n                return Optional.of(Compression.lz4()\n                        .level(getInt(TopicConfig.COMPRESSION_LZ4_LEVEL_CONFIG))\n                        .build());\n            case ZSTD:\n                return Optional.of(Compression.zstd()\n                        .level(getInt(TopicConfig.COMPRESSION_ZSTD_LEVEL_CONFIG))\n                        .build());\n            case SNAPPY:\n                return Optional.of(Compression.snappy().build());\n ConfigException(TopicConfig.LOCAL_LOG_RETENTION_BYTES_CONFIG, localRetentionBytes, message);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static void validateRemoteStorageRetentionTime(Map<?, ?>
